       </section>\r\n    </div>\r\n\r\n    <script>\r\n        // ===== ê³µí†µ ìœ í‹¸ =====\r\n        function setMetric(id, value) {\r\n            const el = document.getElementById(id);\r\n            if (!el) return;\r\n\r\n            el.classList.remove(\"positive\", \"negative\");\r\n\r\n            if (id === \"m-symbol\" || id === \"m-price\" || id === \"m-equity\") {\r\n                el.textContent = value;\r\n                return;\r\n            }\r\n\r\n            if (id === \"maxdd\") {\r\n                el.style.color = \"#000000\";\r\n                if (typeof value === \"string\" && value.startsWith(\"-\")) {\r\n                    el.style.color = \"#d00000\";\r\n                }\r\n                el.textContent = value;\r\n                return;\r\n            }\r\n\r\n            if (typeof value === \"string\" && value.startsWith(\"-\")) {\r\n                el.classList.add(\"negative\");\r\n            } else if (typeof value === \"string\" && value !== \"-\" && value !== \"0\" && !value.startsWith(\"0.\")) {\r\n                el.classList.add(\"positive\");\r\n            }\r\n            el.textContent = value;\r\n        }\r\n\r\n        function formatNumber(v, digits = 2) {\r\n            if (v === null || v === undefined || isNaN(v)) return \"-\";\r\n            return Number(v).toLocaleString(\"ko-KR\", {\r\n                minimumFractionDigits: digits,\r\n                maximumFractionDigits: digits,\r\n            });\r\n        }\r\n\r\n        function formatPercent(v, digits = 2) {\r\n            if (v === null || v === undefined || isNaN(v)) return \"-\";\r\n            return (Number(v) * 100).toFixed(digits) + \"%\";\r\n        }\r\n\r\n        function formatTimeLabel(ts) {\r\n            try {\r\n                const d = new Date(ts);\r\n                if (isNaN(d.getTime())) return String(ts ?? \"\");\r\n                return d.toLocaleTimeString(\"ko-KR\", {\r\n                    hour12: false,\r\n                    hour: \"2-digit\",\r\n                    minute: \"2-digit\",\r\n                    second: \"2-digit\",\r\n                });\r\n            } catch {\r\n                return String(ts ?? \"\");\r\n            }\r\n        }\r\n\r\n        // ===== íˆìŠ¤í† ë¦¬ ë²„í¼ =====\r\n        let maxPoints = 300;\r\n\r\n        const labelsHist = [];\r\n        const equityHist = [];\r\n        const priceHist = [];\r\n        const posHist = [];\r\n        const ddHist = [];\r\n        const ddWarnHist = [];\r\n        const ddCutHist = [];\r\n        const cumPnlHist = [];\r\n        const buyMarkersHist = [];\r\n        const sellMarkersHist = [];\r\n\r\n        // BUY / SELL ë§ˆì»¤ ê³„ì‚°ìš© ìƒíƒœ\r\n        let lastPos = null;\r\n\r\n        const BUY_MARK_Y = 0.4;\r\n        const SELL_MARK_Y = 0.6;\r\n\r\n        function trimHistoryArrays() {\r\n            const arrays = [\r\n                labelsHist,\r\n                equityHist,\r\n                priceHist,\r\n                posHist,\r\n                ddWarnHist,   // âœ… (ì¶”ê°€)\r\n                ddCutHist,    // âœ… (ì¶”ê°€)\r\n                ddHist,\r\n                cumPnlHist,\r\n                buyMarkersHist,\r\n                sellMarkersHist,\r\n            ];\r\n\r\n            arrays.forEach(arr => {\r\n                if (arr.length > maxPoints) {\r\n                    arr.splice(0, arr.length - maxPoints);\r\n                }\r\n            });\r\n        }\r\n\r\n        function pushHistoryPoint(data) {\r\n            const nowTs = data.ts || data.time || new Date().toISOString();\r\n\r\n            const label = formatTimeLabel(nowTs);\r\n            const price = Number(data.price ?? data.px ?? 0);\r\n            const equity = Number(data.equity ?? data.eq ?? 0);\r\n            const pos = Number(data.position ?? data.pos ?? 0);\r\n            const ddRaw = Number(data.dd ?? data.drawdown ?? 0);\r\n            const cumPnl = Number(data.cum_pnl ?? data.cumpnl ?? data.pnl_cum ?? data.rpnl ?? 0);\r\n\r\n            let ddVal = ddRaw;\r\n            if (Math.abs(ddVal) > 1) ddVal = ddVal / 100.0;\r\n\r\n            labelsHist.push(label);\r\n            priceHist.push(price);\r\n            equityHist.push(equity);\r\n            posHist.push(pos);\r\n            ddHist.push(ddVal);\r\n\r\n            ddWarnHist.push(Number(data.dd_warn ?? 0));\r\n            ddCutHist.push(Number(data.dd_cut ?? 0));\r\n\r\n            cumPnlHist.push(cumPnl);\r\n\r\n            // ==== BUY/SELL ë§ˆì»¤: í¬ì§€ì…˜ ë³€í™” ê°ì§€ ====\r\n            let buyMark = null;\r\n            let sellMark = null;\r\n\r\n            const EPS = 0.00000001; // ê·¹ì†ŒëŸ‰ ë…¸ì´ì¦ˆëŠ” ë¬´ì‹œ\r\n\r\n            if (lastPos === null) {\r\n                lastPos = pos;\r\n            } else {\r\n                const diffPos = pos - lastPos;\r\n\r\n                if (Math.abs(diffPos) > EPS) {\r\n                    if (diffPos > 0) {\r\n                        buyMark = BUY_MARK_Y;\r\n                    } else {\r\n                        sellMark = SELL_MARK_Y;\r\n                    }\r\n                    lastPos = pos;\r\n                }\r\n            }\r\n\r\n            buyMarkersHist.push(buyMark);\r\n            sellMarkersHist.push(sellMark);\r\n\r\n            trimHistoryArrays();\r\n        }\r\n\r\n        // ===== ì°¨íŠ¸ ê°ì²´ =====\r\n        let mainChart = null;\r\n        let pnlChart = null;\r\n\r\n        // ===== ìŠ¤ëƒ…ìƒ· + ì°¨íŠ¸ ì—…ë°ì´íŠ¸ =====\r\n        function updateSnapshotAndCharts(data) {\r\n            const symbol = data.symbol ?? \"-\";\r\n            const price = data.price ?? null;\r\n            const pos = data.position ?? null;\r\n            const eq = data.equity ?? null;\r\n            const rpnl = data.rpnl ?? 0;\r\n            const upnl = data.upnl ?? 0;\r\n            const dd = data.dd ?? null;\r\n            const maxdd = data.max_dd ?? null;\r\n            const totalPnl = (rpnl || 0) + (upnl || 0);\r\n\r\n            setMetric(\"m-symbol\", symbol);\r\n            setMetric(\"m-price\", formatNumber(price));\r\n            setMetric(\"m-position\", formatNumber(pos, 4));\r\n            setMetric(\"m-equity\", formatNumber(eq));\r\n\r\n            setMetric(\"m-pnl\", formatNumber(totalPnl));\r\n            setMetric(\"m-upnl\", formatNumber(upnl));\r\n            setMetric(\"m-rpnl\", formatNumber(rpnl));\r\n            setMetric(\"m-cumpnl\", formatNumber(data.cum_pnl ?? totalPnl));\r\n\r\n            setMetric(\"m-dd\", formatPercent(dd));\r\n            setMetric(\"maxdd\", formatPercent(maxdd));\r\n\r\n            const lu = document.getElementById(\"last-updated\");\r\n            if (lu) {\r\n                lu.textContent =\r\n                    \"Last update: \" +\r\n                    new Date().toLocaleTimeString(\"ko-KR\", {\r\n                        hour12: false,\r\n                        hour: \"2-digit\",\r\n                        minute: \"2-digit\",\r\n                        second: \"2-digit\",\r\n                    });\r\n            }\r\n\r\n            // íˆìŠ¤í† ë¦¬ + ì°¨íŠ¸ ë°˜ì˜\r\n            pushHistoryPoint(data);\r\n\r\n            if (!mainChart || !pnlChart) return;\r\n\r\n            mainChart.data.labels = [...labelsHist];\r\n            mainChart.data.datasets[0].data = [...equityHist];\r\n            mainChart.data.datasets[1].data = [...priceHist];\r\n            mainChart.data.datasets[2].data = [...cumPnlHist];\r\n            mainChart.data.datasets[3].data = [...buyMarkersHist];\r\n            mainChart.data.datasets[4].data = [...sellMarkersHist];\r\n            mainChart.update();\r\n\r\n            pnlChart.data.labels = [...labelsHist];\r\n            pnlChart.data.datasets[0].data = [...posHist];\r\n            pnlChart.data.datasets[1].data = [...ddHist];\r\n\r\n            // âœ… DD_WARN / DD_CUT ê¸°ì¤€ì„ (ê³ ì • ìˆ˜í‰ì„ ) ìƒì„±\r\n            const _rp = (window.riskProfilesByKey && window.uiActiveKey) ? window.riskProfilesByKey[window.uiActiveKey] : null;\r\n            const _ddWarnValue = (_rp?.DD_WARN ?? window.activeRiskProfile?.DD_WARN ?? -0.002);\r\n            const _ddCutValue = (_rp?.DD_CUT ?? window.activeRiskProfile?.DD_CUT ?? -0.010);\r\n\r\n            const _ddWarnLine = labelsHist.map(() => _ddWarnValue);\r\n            const _ddCutLine = labelsHist.map(() => _ddCutValue);\r\n\r\n            pnlChart.data.datasets[2].data = _ddWarnLine;  // label: \"DD_WARN\"\r\n            pnlChart.data.datasets[3].data = _ddCutLine;   // label: \"DD_CUT\"\r\n\r\n            pnlChart.update();\r\n\r\n        }\r\n\r\n        // ===== ë¦¬ìŠ¤í¬ í”„ë¡œíŒŒì¼ í—¬í¼ =====\r\n        async function fetchRiskProfileStatus() {\r\n            try {\r\n                const resp = await fetch(\"/api/risk-profile/active\");\r\n                if (!resp.ok) {\r\n                    console.error(\"[RISK_PROFILE] fetch ì‹¤íŒ¨\", resp.status);\r\n                    return null;\r\n                }\r\n                return await resp.json();\r\n\r\n            } catch (err) {\r\n                console.error(\"[RISK_PROFILE] fetch ì—ëŸ¬\", err);\r\n                return null;\r\n            }\r\n        }\r\n\r\n        const select = document.getElementById(\"risk-profile-select\");\r\n        const label = document.getElementById(\"active-risk-profile\");\r\n\r\n        // 1) ì—”ì§„ ê¸°ì¤€ì´ â€œì§„ì§œ ê°’â€\r\n        const engineActive =\r\n            data.engine_active_profile ||\r\n            \"neutral\";\r\n\r\n        // 2) UI ê°’ì€ ì—”ì§„ ì—†ì„ ë•Œë§Œ ë³´ì¡°ë¡œ ì‚¬ìš©\r\n        const uiActive = data.ui_active_profile || engineActive;\r\n\r\n        window.uiActiveKey = uiActive;                 // âœ… ì—¬ê¸°ë¡œ ì´ë™\r\n        window.riskProfilesByKey = data.profiles || {};\r\n\r\n        // ğŸ”¹ ì½¤ë³´ë°•ìŠ¤ëŠ” í•­ìƒ ì—”ì§„ ê°’ì— ë§ì¶˜ë‹¤\r\n        if (select) {\r\n            select.value = engineActive;\r\n        }\r\n\r\n        // ğŸ”¹ ë¼ë²¨ë„ ì—”ì§„ ê°’ ê¸°ì¤€ìœ¼ë¡œ í‘œì‹œ\r\n        if (label) {\r\n            const nameMap = {\r\n                conservative: \"ë³´ìˆ˜í˜•\",\r\n                neutral: \"ì¤‘ë¦½í˜•\",\r\n                aggressive: \"ê³µê²©í˜•\",\r\n            };\r\n            label.textContent =\r\n                `í˜„ì¬ í”„ë¡œíŒŒì¼: ${nameMap[engineActive] || engineActive}`;\r\n        }\r\n\r\n        // âœ… í”„ë¡œí•„ ë³€ê²½ ì‹œ DD_WARN/DD_CUT ê¸°ì¤€ì„  ì¦‰ì‹œ ê°±ì‹  (í•¨ìˆ˜ ì¢…ë£Œ ì§ì „)\r\n        if (pnlChart) {\r\n            const _labels = pnlChart.data.labels || [];\r\n            const _ddWarnValue = (window.activeRiskProfile?.DD_WARN ?? -0.002);\r\n            const _ddCutValue = (window.activeRiskProfile?.DD_CUT ?? -0.010);\r\n            pnlChart.data.datasets[2].data = _labels.map(() => _ddWarnValue); // DD_WARN\r\n            pnlChart.data.datasets[3].data = _labels.map(() => _ddCutValue);  // DD_CUT\r\n            pnlChart.update();\r\n        }\r\n\r\n        // ===== ìŠ¤ëƒ…ìƒ· ìƒˆë¡œê³ ì¹¨ =====\r\n        async function refreshSnapshot() {\r\n            try {\r\n                const res = await fetch(\"/api/snapshot\");\r\n                if (!res.ok) throw new Error(\"snapshot http \" + res.status);\r\n\r\n                const data = await res.json();\r\n                window.snapshot_last = data\r\n                window.activeRiskProfile = data;\r\n\r\n                const banner = document.getElementById(\"alert-banner\");\r\n                const snap = document.querySelector(\"section.card.snapshot\");\r\n\r\n                if (!banner || !snap) return;   // âœ… ì—¬ê¸° ì¶”ê°€ (banner.className ì „ì—)\r\n\r\n\r\n                // âœ… cut-soon(âš ï¸ë¦¬ìŠ¤í¬ ê´€ë¦¬ ëŒ€ê¸° ì¤‘): FLAT(í¬ì§€ì…˜ 0)ì¼ ë•Œë§Œ í‘œì‹œ\r\n                const cutSoonEl = document.getElementById(\"cut-soon\");\r\n                if (cutSoonEl) {\r\n                    const pos = Number(data.position ?? 0);\r\n                    const shouldShow = Math.abs(pos) < 1e-12; // FLAT\r\n                    cutSoonEl.classList.toggle(\"hidden\", !shouldShow);\r\n                }\r\n\r\n                banner.className = \"alert-banner hidden\";\r\n                snap.classList.remove(\"warn-border\", \"cut-border\");\r\n\r\n                if (data.alert_level === \"WARN\") {\r\n                    banner.textContent = \"âš  DD WARN\";\r\n                    banner.classList.remove(\"hidden\");\r\n                    banner.classList.add(\"warn\");\r\n                    snap.classList.add(\"warn-border\");\r\n                }\r\n\r\n                if (data.alert_level === \"CUT\") {\r\n                    banner.textContent = \"ğŸš¨ DD CUT\";\r\n                    banner.classList.remove(\"hidden\");\r\n                    banner.classList.add(\"cut\");\r\n                    snap.classList.add(\"cut-border\");\r\n                }\r\n\r\n\r\n                const level = (data.alert_level || \"OK\").toUpperCase();\r\n                const cls =\r\n                    level === \"CUT\" ? \"level-cut\" :\r\n                        level === \"WARN\" ? \"level-warn\" :\r\n                            \"level-ok\";\r\n\r\n                [\"m-dd\", \"m-dd-warn\", \"m-dd-cut\", \"m-alert-level\"].forEach(id => {\r\n                    const el = document.getElementById(id);\r\n                    if (!el) return;\r\n                    el.classList.remove(\"level-ok\", \"level-warn\", \"level-cut\");\r\n                    el.classList.add(cls);\r\n                });\r\n\r\n                // âœ… í•„ìš”í•˜ë©´ ë‹¤ë¥¸ ê³³ì—ì„œ ì¨ë„ ë˜ë„ë¡ ì „ì—­ì— ì €ì¥\r\n                window.snapshot_last = data;\r\n\r\n                // ğŸ”¢ DD / WARN / CUT / ALERT ê°’ ì„¸íŒ…\r\n                document.getElementById(\"m-dd\").innerText =\r\n                    (data.dd * 100).toFixed(2) + \"%\";\r\n\r\n                document.getElementById(\"m-dd-warn\").innerText =\r\n                    (data.dd_warn * 100).toFixed(2) + \"%\";\r\n\r\n                document.getElementById(\"m-dd-cut\").innerText =\r\n                    (data.dd_cut * 100).toFixed(2) + \"%\";\r\n\r\n                document.getElementById(\"m-alert-level\").innerText =\r\n                    data.alert_level || \"-\";\r\n\r\n\r\n                // ìƒë‹¨ ì¹´ë“œ + ì°¨íŠ¸ ê°±ì‹ \r\n                updateSnapshotAndCharts(data);\r\n\r\n                // âœ… FLAT ìƒíƒœì¼ ë•Œë§Œ \"ë¦¬ìŠ¤í¬ ê´€ë¦¬ ëŒ€ê¸° ì¤‘\" í‘œì‹œ\r\n                if (cutSoonEl) {\r\n                    const pos = Number(data.position ?? 0);\r\n                    const shouldShow = Math.abs(pos) < 1e-12; // FLAT\r\n                    cutSoonEl.classList.toggle(\"hidden\", !shouldShow);\r\n                }\r\n\r\n                // âœ… ë¹„ìš© íŒ¨ë„ì€ ì „ì²´ ìŠ¤ëƒ…ìƒ·(data)ì„ ë„˜ê¸´ë‹¤\r\n                updateCostMetricsPanel(data);\r\n\r\n            } catch (err) {\r\n                console.error(\"snapshot error\", err);\r\n                const lu = document.getElementById(\"last-updated\");\r\n                if (lu) lu.textContent = \"ìŠ¤ëƒ…ìƒ· ì˜¤ë¥˜\";\r\n            }\r\n        }\r\n\r\n\r\n        // ===== ë¹„ìš© íŒ¨ë„ ì—…ë°ì´íŠ¸ =====\r\n        function updateCostMetricsPanel(snapshot) {\r\n            if (!snapshot) return;\r\n\r\n            // âœ… ìŠ¤ëƒ…ìƒ·ì—ì„œ cost_metrics êº¼ë‚´ê¸°\r\n            const cm = snapshot.cost_metrics || {};\r\n\r\n            function put(id, value, digits = 2) {\r\n                const el = document.getElementById(id);\r\n                if (!el) return;\r\n                if (value === null || value === undefined || isNaN(value)) {\r\n                    el.textContent = \"-\";\r\n                    return;\r\n                }\r\n                el.textContent = Number(value).toFixed(digits);\r\n            }\r\n\r\n            // âœ… ìµœê·¼ Nê±´ í‰ê·  ê°œìˆ˜ N (ì„¤ì • íŒŒì¼ì˜ cost_window ìš°ì„ , ì—†ìœ¼ë©´ ë‚´ë¶€ maxlen)\r\n            const nWindow =\r\n                snapshot.cost_window ??\r\n                cm.rolling_window_maxlen ??\r\n                0;\r\n            put(\"cost-rolling-size\", nWindow, 0);\r\n            put(\"m-risk-mult\", snapshot.risk_mult, 4);\r\n            put(\"m-dyn-max-pos\", snapshot.dyn_max_pos, 6);\r\n\r\n            // ìµœê·¼ ì²´ê²°\r\n            put(\"cost-last-total\", cm.last_total_cost_bps, 2);\r\n            put(\"cost-last-slippage\", cm.last_slippage_bps, 2);\r\n            put(\"cost-last-fee\", cm.last_fee_bps, 2);\r\n\r\n            // ì„¸ì…˜ ëˆ„ì \r\n            put(\"cost-session-total-sum\", cm.session_total_cost_sum, 2);\r\n            put(\"cost-session-slip-sum\", cm.session_slippage_sum, 2);\r\n            put(\"cost-session-fee-sum\", cm.session_fee_sum, 2);\r\n            put(\"cost-session-trade-count\", cm.session_trade_count, 0);\r\n\r\n            // ìµœê·¼ Nê±´ í‰ê· \r\n            put(\"cost-rolling-total\", cm.rolling_total_cost_bps, 2);\r\n            put(\"cost-rolling-slip\", cm.rolling_slippage_bps, 2);\r\n            put(\"cost-rolling-fee\", cm.rolling_fee_bps, 2);\r\n        }\r\n\r\n\r\n        // ===== window load =====\r\n        window.addEventListener(\"load\", async () => {\r\n            // ğŸ”¹ ë¦¬ìŠ¤í¬ í”„ë¡œíŒŒì¼ ì½¤ë³´ DOM\r\n            const riskSelect =       // 2) ì‚¬ìš©ìê°€ ì½¤ë³´ë¥¼ ë°”ê¿€ ë•Œ ì„œë²„ì— ë°˜ì˜\r\n            if (riskSelect) {\r\n                riskSelect.addEventListener(\"change\", async (event) => {\r\n                    const                 method: \"POST\",\r\n                            headers: { \"Content-Type\": \"application/json\" },\r\n                            body: JSON.stringify({ profile }),\r\n                        });\r\n\r\n                        if (!resp.ok) {\r\n                            console.error(\"[RISK_PROFILE] update ì‹¤íŒ¨\", resp.status);\r\n                            return;\r\n                        }\r\n\r\n                        const data = await resp.json();\r\n                        console.log(\"[RISK_PROFILE] updated:\", data);\r\n\r\n                        // ë³€ê²½         pnlChart.update();\r\n                    } catch (err) {\r\n                        console.error(\"[RISK_PROFILE] update ì—ëŸ¬\", err);\r\n                    }\r\n                });\r\n                await refreshRiskProfileUI();\r\n            }\r\n\r\n            // ===== ì•„ë˜ë¶€í„°ëŠ” ê¸°ì¡´ ì°¨íŠ¸/ë²„íŠ¼ ì´ˆê¸°í™” =====\r\n\r\n            const mainCanvas =          // ê¸°ê°„ ë²„íŠ¼\r\n            const rangeButtons = document.querySelectorAll(\".range-buttons button\");\r\n            let currentRange = \"today\";\r\n            rangeButtons.forEach(btn => {\r\n                btn.addEventListener(\"click\", () => {\r\n                    rangeButtons.forEach(b => b.classList.remove(\"active\"));\r\n                    btn.classList.add(\"active\");\r\n                    currentRange = btn.getAttribute(\"data-range\") || \"today\";\r\n                    console.log(\"ğŸ“Œ range changed:\", currentRange);\r\n                });\r\n            });\r\n\r\n            // íˆìŠ¤í† ë¦¬ ê¸¸ì´\r\n            const maxPointsSelect = document.getElementById(\"maxPointsSelect\");\r\n            if (maxPointsSelect) {\r\n                maxPointsSelect.value = String(maxPoints);\r\n                maxPointsSelect.addEventListener(\"change\", () => {\r\n                    const v = parseInt(maxPointsSelect.value, 10);\r\n                    if (!isNaN(v) && v > 0) {\r\n                        maxPoints = v;\r\n                        trimHistoryArrays();\r\n                        if (mainChart && pnlChart) {\r\n                            mainChart.update();\r\n                            pnlChart.update();\r\n                        }\r\n                    }\r\n                });\r\n                await refreshRiskProfileUI();\r\n            }\r\n\r\n            // ìƒë‹¨ ë©”ì¸ ì°¨íŠ¸\r\n            mainChart = new Chart(mainCtx, {\r\n                type: \"line\",\r\n                data:                          pointStyle: \"circle\",\r\n                            pointBackgroundColor: \"#000000\"\r\n                        },\r\n                        {\r\n         pointStyle: \"triangle\",\r\n                            rotation: 0,\r\n                            pointBorderWidth: 2,\r\n                            showLine: false,\r\n                            spanGaps: true,\r\n                        },\r\n                        {\r\n                            label: \"Sell\",\r\n                            data: [],\r\n                    pointStyle: \"triangle\",\r\n                            rotation: 180,\r\n                            pointBorderWidth: 2,\r\n                            showLine: false,\r\n                            spanGaps: true,\r\n                        },\r\n                    ],\r\n                },\r\n                options: {\r\n                    responsive: true,\r\n                                Number(value).toLocaleString(\"ko-KR\", {\r\n                                        minimumFractionDigits: 2,\r\n                                        maximumFractionDigits: 2,\r\n                                    }),\r\n                            },\r\n                        },\r\n                        yCumPnl: {\r\n                <span class=\"metric-value\" id=\"cost-rolling-size\">-</span>\r\n                </div>\r\n            </section>\r\n        </div>\r\n\r\n        <!-- ë©”ì¸ ê·¸ë˜í”„ ì¹´ë“œ -->\r\n        <section class=\"card chart-card\">\r\n            <div class=\"chart-header\">\r\n                Price Â· Equity Â· BUY/SELL (ìƒë‹¨ ë©”ì¸ì°¨íŠ¸)\r\n            </div>\r\n            <div class=\"chart-controls\">\r\n                <div class=\"range-buttons\">\r\n                    <button type=\"button\" data-range=\"today\" class=\"active\">ì˜¤ëŠ˜</button>\r\n                    <button type=\"button\" data-range=\"1h\">1ì‹œê°„</button>\r\n                    <button type=\"button\" data-range=\"3h\">3ì‹œê°„</button>\r\n                </div>\r\n                <div class=\"history-select\">\r\n                    <label for=\"maxPointsSelect\">í‘œì‹œ êµ¬ê°„:</label>\r\n                    <select id=\"maxPointsSelect\">\r\n                        <option value=\"300\">5ë¶„ (300)</option>\r\n                        <option value=\"600\">10ë¶„ (600)</option>\r\n                        <option value=\"1200\">20ë¶„ (1200)</option>\r\n                        <option value=\"1800\">30ë¶„ (1800)</option>\r\n                    </select>\r\n                </div>\r\n            </div>\r\n\r\n            <div class=\"chart-row chart-row-main\">\r\n                <canvas id=\"mainChart\"></canvas>\r\n            </div>\r\n\r\n            <div class=\"chart-row chart-row-pnl\">\r\n                <canvas id=\"pnlChart\"></canvas>\r\n            </div>\r\n        </section>\r\n    </div>\r\n\r\n    <script>\r\n        // ===== ê³µí†µ ìœ í‹¸ =====\r\n        function setMetric(id, value) {\r\n            const el = document.getElementById(id);\r\n            if (!el) return;\r\n\r\n            el.classList.remove(\"positive\", \"negative\");\r\n\r\n            if (id === \"m-symbol\" || id === \"m-price\" || id === \"m-equity\") {\r\n                el.textContent = value;\r\n                return;\r\n            }\r\n\r\n            if (id === \"maxdd\") {\r\n                el.style.color = \"#000000\";\r\n                if (typeof value === \"string\" && value.startsWith(\"-\")) {\r\n                    el.style.color = \"#d00000\";\r\n                }\r\n                el.textContent = value;\r\n                return;\r\n            }\r\n\r\n            if (typeof value === \"string\" && value.startsWith(\"-\")) {\r\n                el.classList.add(\"negative\");\r\n            } else if (typeof value === \"string\" && value !== \"-\" && value !== \"0\" && !value.startsWith(\"0.\")) {\r\n                el.classList.add(\"positive\");\r\n            }\r\n            el.textContent = value;\r\n        }\r\n\r\n        function formatNumber(v, digits = 2) {\r\n            if (v === null || v === undefined || isNaN(v)) return \"-\";\r\n            return Number(v).toLocaleString(\"ko-KR\", {\r\n                minimumFractionDigits: digits,\r\n                maximumFractionDigits: digits,\r\n            });\r\n        }\r\n\r\n        function formatPercent(v, digits = 2) {\r\n            if (v === null || v === undefined || isNaN(v)) return \"-\";\r\n            return (Number(v) * 100).toFixed(digits) + \"%\";\r\n        }\r\n\r\n        function formatTimeLabel(ts) {\r\n            try {\r\n                const d = new Date(ts);\r\n                if (isNaN(d.getTime())) return String(ts ?? \"\");\r\n                return d.toLocaleTimeString(\"ko-KR\", {\r\n                    hour12: false,\r\n                    hour: \"2-digit\",\r\n                    minute: \"2-digit\",\r\n                    second: \"2-digit\",\r\n                });\r\n            } catch {\r\n                return String(ts ?? \"\");\r\n            }\r\n        }\r\n\r\n        // ===== íˆìŠ¤í† ë¦¬ ë²„í¼ =====\r\n        let maxPoints = 300;\r\n\r\n        const labelsHist = [];\r\n        const equityHist = [];\r\n        const priceHist = [];\r\n        const posHist = [];\r\n        const ddHist = [];\r\n        const ddWarnHist = [];\r\n        const ddCutHist = [];\r\n        const cumPnlHist = [];\r\n        const buyMarkersHist = [];\r\n        const sellMarkersHist = [];\r\n\r\n        // BUY / SELL ë§ˆì»¤ ê³„ì‚°ìš© ìƒíƒœ\r\n        let lastPos = null;\r\n\r\n        const BUY_MARK_Y = 0.4;\r\n        const SELL_MARK_Y = 0.6;\r\n\r\n        function trimHistoryArrays() {\r\n            const arrays = [\r\n                labelsHist,\r\n                equityHist,\r\n                priceHist,\r\n                posHist,\r\n                ddWarnHist,   // âœ… (ì¶”ê°€)\r\n                ddCutHist,    // âœ… (ì¶”ê°€)\r\n                ddHist,\r\n                cumPnlHist,\r\n                buyMarkersHist,\r\n                sellMarkersHist,\r\n            ];\r\n\r\n            arrays.forEach(arr => {\r\n                if (arr.length > maxPoints) {\r\n                    arr.splice(0, arr.length - maxPoints);\r\n                }\r\n            });\r\n        }\r\n\r\n        function pushHistoryPoint(data) {\r\n            const nowTs = data.ts || data.time || new Date().toISOString();\r\n\r\n            const label = formatTimeLabel(nowTs);\r\n            const price = Number(data.price ?? data.px ?? 0);\r\n            const equity = Number(data.equity ?? data.eq ?? 0);\r\n            const pos = Number(data.position ?? data.pos ?? 0);\r\n            const ddRaw = Number(data.dd ?? data.drawdown ?? 0);\r\n            const cumPnl = Number(data.cum_pnl ?? data.cumpnl ?? data.pnl_cum ?? data.rpnl ?? 0);\r\n\r\n            let ddVal = ddRaw;\r\n            if (Math.abs(ddVal) > 1) ddVal = ddVal / 100.0;\r\n\r\n            labelsHist.push(label);\r\n            priceHist.push(price);\r\n            equityHist.push(equity);\r\n            posHist.push(pos);\r\n            ddHist.push(ddVal);\r\n\r\n            ddWarnHist.push(Number(data.dd_warn ?? 0));\r\n            ddCutHist.push(Number(data.dd_cut ?? 0));\r\n\r\n            cumPnlHist.push(cumPnl);\r\n\r\n            // ==== BUY/SELL ë§ˆì»¤: í¬ì§€ì…˜ ë³€í™” ê°ì§€ ====\r\n            let buyMark = null;\r\n            let sellMark = null;\r\n\r\n            const EPS = 0.00000001; // ê·¹ì†ŒëŸ‰ ë…¸ì´ì¦ˆëŠ” ë¬´ì‹œ\r\n\r\n            if (lastPos === null) {\r\n                lastPos = pos;\r\n            } else {\r\n                const diffPos = pos - lastPos;\r\n\r\n                if (Math.abs(diffPos) > EPS) {\r\n                    if (diffPos > 0) {\r\n                        buyMark = BUY_MARK_Y;\r\n                    } else {\r\n                        sellMark = SELL_MARK_Y;\r\n                    }\r\n                    lastPos = pos;\r\n                }\r\n            }\r\n\r\n            buyMarkersHist.push(buyMark);\r\n            sellMarkersHist.push(sellMark);\r\n\r\n            trimHistoryArrays();\r\n        }\r\n\r\n        // ===== ì°¨íŠ¸ ê°ì²´ =====\r\n        let mainChart = null;\r\n        let pnlChart = null;\r\n\r\n        // ===== ìŠ¤ëƒ…ìƒ· + ì°¨íŠ¸ ì—…ë°ì´íŠ¸ =====\r\n        function updateSnapshotAndCharts(data) {\r\n            const symbol = data.symbol ?? \"-\";\r\n            const price = data.price ?? null;\r\n            const pos = data.position ?? null;\r\n            const eq = data.equity ?? null;\r\n            const rpnl = data.rpnl ?? 0;\r\n            const upnl = data.upnl ?? 0;\r\n            const dd = data.dd ?? null;\r\n            const maxdd = data.max_dd ?? null;\r\n            const totalPnl = (rpnl || 0) + (upnl || 0);\r\n\r\n            setMetric(\"m-symbol\", symbol);\r\n            setMetric(\"m-price\", formatNumber(price));\r\n            setMetric(\"m-position\", formatNumber(pos, 4));\r\n            setMetric(\"m-equity\", formatNumber(eq));\r\n\r\n            setMetric(\"m-pnl\", formatNumber(totalPnl));\r\n            setMetric(\"m-upnl\", formatNumber(upnl));\r\n            setMetric(\"m-rpnl\", formatNumber(rpnl));\r\n            setMetric(\"m-cumpnl\", formatNumber(data.cum_pnl ?? totalPnl));\r\n\r\n            setMetric(\"m-dd\", formatPercent(dd));\r\n            setMetric(\"maxdd\", formatPercent(maxdd));\r\n\r\n            const lu = document.getElementById(\"last-updated\");\r\n            if (lu) {\r\n                lu.textContent =\r\n                    \"Last update: \" +\r\n                    new Date().toLocaleTimeString(\"ko-KR\", {\r\n                        hour12: false,\r\n                        hour: \"2-digit\",\r\n                        minute: \"2-digit\",\r\n                        second: \"2-digit\",\r\n                    });\r\n            }\r\n\r\n            // íˆìŠ¤í† ë¦¬ + ì°¨íŠ¸ ë°˜ì˜\r\n            pushHistoryPoint(data);\r\n\r\n            if (!mainChart || !pnlChart) return;\r\n\r\n            mainChart.data.labels = [...labelsHist];\r\n            mainChart.data.datasets[0].data = [...equityHist];\r\n            mainChart.data.datasets[1].data = [...priceHist];\r\n            mainChart.data.datasets[2].data = [...cumPnlHist];\r\n            mainChart.data.datasets[3].data = [...buyMarkersHist];\r\n            mainChart.data.datasets[4].data = [...sellMarkersHist];\r\n            mainChart.update();\r\n\r\n            pnlChart.data.labels = [...labelsHist];\r\n            pnlChart.data.datasets[0].data = [...posHist];\r\n            pnlChart.data.datasets[1].data = [...ddHist];\r\n\r\n            // âœ… DD_WARN / DD_CUT ê¸°ì¤€ì„ (ê³ ì • ìˆ˜í‰ì„ ) ìƒì„±\r\n            const _rp = (window.riskProfilesByKey && window.uiActiveKey) ? window.riskProfilesByKey[window.uiActiveKey] : null;\r\n            const _ddWarnValue = (_rp?.DD_WARN ?? window.activeRiskProfile?.DD_WARN ?? -0.002);\r\n            const _ddCutValue = (_rp?.DD_CUT ?? window.activeRiskProfile?.DD_CUT ?? -0.010);\r\n\r\n            const _ddWarnLine = labelsHist.map(() => _ddWarnValue);\r\n            const _ddCutLine = labelsHist.map(() => _ddCutValue);\r\n\r\n            pnlChart.data.datasets[2].data = _ddWarnLine;  // label: \"DD_WARN\"\r\n            pnlChart.data.datasets[3].data = _ddCutLine;   // label: \"DD_CUT\"\r\n\r\n            pnlChart.update();\r\n\r\n        }\r\n\r\n        // ===== ë¦¬ìŠ¤í¬ í”„ë¡œíŒŒì¼ í—¬í¼ =====\r\n        async function fetchRiskProfileStatus() {\r\n            try {\r\n                const resp = await fetch(\"/api/risk-profile/active\");\r\n                if (!resp.ok) {\r\n                    console.error(\"[RISK_PROFILE] fetch ì‹¤íŒ¨\", resp.status);\r\n                    return null;\r\n                }\r\n                return await resp.json();\r\n\r\n            } catch (err) {\r\n                console.error(\"[RISK_PROFILE] fetch ì—ëŸ¬\", err);\r\n                return null;\r\n            }\r\n        }\r\n\r\n        // ===== ë¦¬ìŠ¤í¬ í”„ë¡œíŒŒì¼ UI ë™ê¸°í™”(ì •ì„) =====\r\n        async function refreshRiskProfileUI() {\r\n            const data = await fetchRiskProfileStatus();\r\n            if (!data) return;\r\n\r\n            const engineActive = data.engine_active_profile || \"neutral\";\r\n            const uiActive = engineActive;\r\n\r\n            // ì „ì—­ ìƒíƒœ(ë‹¨ì¼ ê¸°ì¤€)\r\n            window.riskProfilesByKey = data.profiles || {};\r\n            window.uiActiveKey = uiActive;\r\n            window.activeRiskProfile = window.riskProfilesByKey[uiActive] || null;\r\n\r\n            // ì½¤ë³´/ë¼ë²¨ ë™ê¸°í™”\r\n            if (select) select.value = engineActive;\r\n\r\n            if (label) {\r\n                const nameMap = { conservative: \"ë³´ìˆ˜í˜•\", neutral: \"ì¤‘ë¦½í˜•\", aggressive: \"ê³µê²©í˜•\" };\r\n                label.textContent = `í˜„ì¬ í”„ë¡œíŒŒì¼: ${nameMap[engineActive] || engineActive}`;\r\n            }\r\n\r\n            // DD ë¼ì¸ ì¦‰ì‹œ ê°±ì‹ (ì°¨íŠ¸ ì¡´ì¬í•  ë•Œë§Œ)\r\n            if (pnlChart) {\r\n                const _labels = pnlChart.data.labels || [];\r\n                const w = window.activeRiskProfile?.DD_WARN ?? -0.002;\r\n                const c = window.activeRiskProfile?.DD_CUT ?? -0.010;\r\n                pnlChart.data.datasets[2].data = _labels.map(() => w);\r\n                pnlChart.data.datasets[3].data = _labels.map(() => c);\r\n                pnlChart.update();\r\n            }\r\n        }\r\n\r\n        // ğŸ”¹ ì½¤ë³´ë°•ìŠ¤ëŠ” í•­ìƒ ì—”ì§„ ê°’ì— ë§ì¶˜ë‹¤\r\n        if (select) {\r\n            select.value = engineActive;\r\n        }\r\n\r\n        // ğŸ”¹ ë¼ë²¨ë„ ì—”ì§„ ê°’ ê¸°ì¤€ìœ¼ë¡œ í‘œì‹œ\r\n        if (label) {\r\n            const nameMap = {\r\n                conservative: \"ë³´ìˆ˜í˜•\",\r\n                neutral: \"ì¤‘ë¦½í˜•\",\r\n                aggressive: \"ê³µê²©í˜•\",\r\n            };\r\n            label.textContent =\r\n                `í˜„ì¬ í”„ë¡œíŒŒì¼: ${nameMap[engineActive] || engineActive}`;\r\n        }\r\n\r\n        // âœ… í”„ë¡œí•„ ë³€ê²½ ì‹œ DD_WARN/DD_CUT ê¸°ì¤€ì„  ì¦‰ì‹œ ê°±ì‹  (í•¨ìˆ˜ ì¢…ë£Œ ì§ì „)\r\n        if (pnlChart) {\r\n            const _labels = pnlChart.data.labels || [];\r\n            const _ddWarnValue = (window.activeRiskProfile?.DD_WARN ?? -0.002);\r\n            const _ddCutValue = (window.activeRiskProfile?.DD_CUT ?? -0.010);\r\n            pnlChart.data.datasets[2].data = _labels.map(() => _ddWarnValue); // DD_WARN\r\n            pnlChart.data.datasets[3].data = _labels.map(() => _ddCutValue);  // DD_CUT\r\n            pnlChart.update();\r\n        }\r\n\r\n        // ===== ìŠ¤ëƒ…ìƒ· ìƒˆë¡œê³ ì¹¨ =====\r\n        async function refreshSnapshot() {\r\n            try {\r\n                const res = await fetch(\"/api/snapshot\");\r\n                if (!res.ok) throw new Error(\"snapshot http \" + res.status);\r\n\r\n                const data = await res.json();\r\n                window.snapshot_last = data\r\n\r\n                const banner = document.getElementById(\"alert-banner\");\r\n                const snap = document.querySelector(\"section.card.snapshot\");\r\n\r\n                if (!banner || !snap) return;   // âœ… ì—¬ê¸° ì¶”ê°€ (banner.className ì „ì—)\r\n\r\n\r\n                // âœ… cut-soon(âš ï¸ë¦¬ìŠ¤í¬ ê´€ë¦¬ ëŒ€ê¸° ì¤‘): FLAT(í¬ì§€ì…˜ 0)ì¼ ë•Œë§Œ í‘œì‹œ\r\n                const cutSoonEl = document.getElementById(\"cut-soon\");\r\n                if (cutSoonEl) {\r\n                    const pos = Number(data.position ?? 0);\r\n                    const shouldShow = Math.abs(pos) < 1e-12; // FLAT\r\n                    cutSoonEl.classList.toggle(\"hidden\", !shouldShow);\r\n                }\r\n\r\n                banner.className = \"alert-banner hidden\";\r\n                snap.classList.remove(\"warn-border\", \"cut-border\");\r\n\r\n                if (data.alert_level === \"WARN\") {\r\n                    banner.textContent = \"âš  DD WARN\";\r\n                    banner.classList.remove(\"hidden\");\r\n                    banner.classList.add(\"warn\");\r\n                    snap.classList.add(\"warn-border\");\r\n                }\r\n\r\n                if (data.alert_level === \"CUT\") {\r\n                    banner.textContent = \"ğŸš¨ DD CUT\";\r\n                    banner.classList.remove(\"hidden\");\r\n                    banner.classList.add(\"cut\");\r\n                    snap.classList.add(\"cut-border\");\r\n                }\r\n\r\n\r\n                const level = (data.alert_level || \"OK\").toUpperCase();\r\n                const cls =\r\n                    level === \"CUT\" ? \"level-cut\" :\r\n                        level === \"WARN\" ? \"level-warn\" :\r\n                            \"level-ok\";\r\n\r\n                [\"m-dd\", \"m-dd-warn\", \"m-dd-cut\", \"m-alert-level\"].forEach(id => {\r\n                    const el = document.getElementById(id);\r\n                    if (!el) return;\r\n                    el.classList.remove(\"level-ok\", \"level-warn\", \"level-cut\");\r\n                    el.classList.add(cls);\r\n                });\r\n\r\n                // âœ… í•„ìš”í•˜ë©´ ë‹¤ë¥¸ ê³³ì—ì„œ ì¨ë„ ë˜ë„ë¡ ì „ì—­ì— ì €ì¥\r\n                window.snapshot_last = data;\r\n\r\n                // ğŸ”¢ DD / WARN / CUT / ALERT ê°’ ì„¸íŒ…\r\n                document.getElementById(\"m-dd\").innerText =\r\n                    (data.dd * 100).toFixed(2) + \"%\";\r\n\r\n                document.getElementById(\"m-dd-warn\").innerText =\r\n                    (data.dd_warn * 100).toFixed(2) + \"%\";\r\n\r\n                document.getElementById(\"m-dd-cut\").innerText =\r\n                    (data.dd_cut * 100).toFixed(2) + \"%\";\r\n\r\n                document.getElementById(\"m-alert-level\").innerText =\r\n                    data.alert_level || \"-\";\r\n\r\n\r\n                // ìƒë‹¨ ì¹´ë“œ + ì°¨íŠ¸ ê°±ì‹ \r\n                updateSnapshotAndCharts(data);\r\n\r\n                // âœ… FLAT ìƒíƒœì¼ ë•Œë§Œ \"ë¦¬ìŠ¤í¬ ê´€ë¦¬ ëŒ€ê¸° ì¤‘\" í‘œì‹œ\r\n                if (cutSoonEl) {\r\n                    const pos = Number(data.position ?? 0);\r\n                    const shouldShow = Math.abs(pos) < 1e-12; // FLAT\r\n                    cutSoonEl.classList.toggle(\"hidden\", !shouldShow);\r\n                }\r\n\r\n                // âœ… ë¹„ìš© íŒ¨ë„ì€ ì „ì²´ ìŠ¤ëƒ…ìƒ·(data)ì„ ë„˜ê¸´ë‹¤\r\n                updateCostMetricsPanel(data);\r\n\r\n            } catch (err) {\r\n                console.error(\"snapshot error\", err);\r\n                const lu = document.getElementById(\"last-updated\");\r\n
